            <h3 class="PagePromo-title">
                <a class="Link " href="https://apnews.com/article/death-loss-grief-palliative-care-137e76cc917f749cc06879e17c10b5fc"><span class="PagePromoContentIcons-text">Talking about death can be tricky. Heres how to start the conversation</span></a>
            </h3>
        </bsp-custom-headline>
    





        



    <div class="PagePromo-description">
        <a class="Link " href="https://apnews.com/article/death-loss-grief-palliative-care-137e76cc917f749cc06879e17c10b5fc"><span class="PagePromoContentIcons-text">Talking about death is never easy, but doing so early can help families prepare. Experts recommend starting off by asking what matters most to their loved one such as what song they might want played at their funeral, or where theyd like to be buried.</span></a>
    </div>

    <script>function optanCheck () {
     
	var onCookie = document.cookie
    try {
        var theCookie = onCookie.match(/(OptanonConsent=.*;?)/)[0]
        if (typeof OnetrustActiveGroups === 'string' && OnetrustActiveGroups.split(',').indexOf('4') > 0) {
			var consentId = theCookie.match(/(consentId.*?&)/)[0].replace('&','')
            permutive.consent({"opt_in":true,"token": consentId})
        } else {
            permutive.consent({"opt_in":false})
        }
    } catch(err) {
        console.error('oncookieerror', err)
    }
}</script>
